<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt 0pt 0pt 49pt;text-indent:-49pt;"><b>Item 2.02</b>&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;&#xa0;<b>Results of Operations and Financial Condition.</b></div>

<div style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&#xa0;</div>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;text-indent:25pt;">On October 6, 2022, Conagra Brands, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release which contained information on the Company&#8217;s&#xa0;first quarter fiscal&#xa0;2023 financial results. The press release is furnished with this Current Report on Form 8-K as Exhibit 99.1.</div>

<div style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&#xa0;</div>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-variant:normal;text-align:center;margin:0pt;"><font style="text-transform: uppercase; font-size: 12pt;"><b>CONAGRA BRANDS REPORTS <a data-tblloc="66x1" data-tblname="263810" data-tblv="20" id="led263810F2022681657299890245">first</a> QUARTER RESULTS</b></font></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">CHICAGO, <a data-tblloc="85x1" data-tblname="263810" data-tblv="20" id="led263810F2022681657300688953">October 6, 2022</a>&#8212; Today Conagra Brands, Inc. (NYSE: CAG) reported results for the&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="66x1" data-tblname="263810" data-tblv="20" id="led263810F2022681657299913540">first</a> quarter of fiscal year <a data-tblloc="40x1" data-tblname="263810" data-tblv="20" id="led263810F2022681657300438393">2023</a>, which ended on <a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="263812" data-tblv="20" id="led263812F2022681657300060254">August 28, 2022</a>. All comparisons are against the prior-year fiscal period, unless otherwise noted.&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt;"><b><u>CEO Perspective</u></b></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt;">Sean Connolly, president and chief executive officer of Conagra Brands, commented, "The strength of our brands and continued execution of the Conagra Way playbook resulted in strong sales and adjusted operating profit results during the first quarter. We continued to deliver improved service and productivity as we navigate ongoing inflationary pressures and industry-wide supply chain challenges. Our strong start to fiscal 2023 reaffirms our&nbsp;confidence in our outlook for the balance of the fiscal year as we remain focused on generating value for our shareholders."</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Total Company&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="53x1" data-tblname="263810" data-tblv="20" id="led263810F2022681657299993307">First Quarter</a> Results</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">In the quarter, net sales <a data-tblloc="2x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F2022781659986290835">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F2022791660049148270">9.5%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F2022791660049165813">$2.9</a> billion. The&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x7" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F2022791660049183268">increase</a> in net sales primarily reflects:</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">a&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="6x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F2022791660049248360">0.2%</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="6x7" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F2022791660049261993">decrease</a> from the unfavorable impact of foreign exchange; and</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">a&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F2022791660049282727">9.7%</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x7" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F2022791660049309446">increase</a> in organic net sales.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F2022791660049334186">9.7%</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x7" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F2022791660049359561">increase</a> in organic net sales was driven by a&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F2022791660049379536">14.3%</a> improvement in price/mix, which was partially offset by a&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F2022791660049390922">4.6%</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x7" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F2022791660049403285">decrease</a> in volume. Price/mix was driven by the company&#8217;s inflation-driven pricing actions that were reflected in the marketplace throughout the quarter. The volume decrease was primarily a result of the elasticity impact from inflation-driven pricing actions;<font style="color:#333333;"> however, the elasticity impact was favorable to expectations.</font></p>

<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Gross profit&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x5" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660049499647">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x4" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660049508835">7.0%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660049519257">$720</a> million in the quarter, and adjusted gross profit&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x5" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660049823859">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x4" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660049833892">7.1%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660049842458">$723</a> million.&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="55x1" data-tblname="263810" data-tblv="20" id="led263810F2022681657300031982">First quarter</a> gross profit benefited from higher organic net sales and&nbsp;supply chain realized productivity which more than offset&nbsp;the negative impacts of cost of goods sold inflation of 15%, unfavorable operating leverage, and continued&nbsp;elevated supply chain operating costs. Gross margin&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="5x5" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660049875311">decreased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="5x4" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660049885768">58</a> basis points to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="4x4" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660049898776">24.8%</a> in the quarter, and adjusted gross margin&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="7x5" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660049914074">decreased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="7x4" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660049924191">54</a> basis points to <a data-tblloc="6x4" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660049932524">24.9%</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Selling, general, and administrative expense (SG&amp;A), which includes advertising and promotional expense (A&amp;P),&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x5" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660049962754">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x4" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660049972518">139.1%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660049981591">$742</a> million in the qu<font style="color:#333333;">arter&nbsp;</font>primarily due&nbsp;to $386 million of non-cash goodwill and&nbsp;brand&nbsp;impairment&nbsp;charges. These charges were largely driven by an increased&nbsp;discount rate&nbsp;given&nbsp;the current interest rate environment. Adjusted SG&amp;A, which excludes A&amp;P,&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x5" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660049996959">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x4" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660050005761">10.5%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660050019689">$263</a> million driven b<font style="color:#333333;">y increased incentive compensation compared to&nbsp;the prior year quarter.</font></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">A&amp;P expense of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="10x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660050063043">$62</a> million in the quarter was flat to the prior year period.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Net interest expense was&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="263814" data-tblv="20" id="led263814F2022791660050151152">$97</a> million in the quarter. Compared to the prior-year period, net interest expense&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x6" data-tblname="263814" data-tblv="20" id="led263814F2022791660050170543">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x5" data-tblname="263814" data-tblv="20" id="led263814F2022791660050179416">3.0%</a> or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x3" data-tblname="263814" data-tblv="20" id="led263814F2022791660050187647">$3</a> m<font style="color:#333333;">illion, primarily due to a higher weighted average interest rate on outstanding debt.</font></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The average diluted share count in the quarter was&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="263814" data-tblv="20" id="led263814F2022791660050327584">481</a> million shares. During the first quarter, the Company repurchased approximately 1.4&nbsp;million shares of its common stock for approximately $50 million.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; margin: 0pt; text-align: left;">In the quarter, net loss attributable to Conagra Brands was&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="11x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660050393587">$78</a> million, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="13x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660050408870">$0.16</a> per diluted share. Adjusted net income attributable to Conagra Brands&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="12x5" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660050427061">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="12x4" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660051208036">14.2%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="12x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660051216702">$275</a> million, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="14x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F2022791660051225596">$0.57</a> per diluted share. The increase was&nbsp;driven primarily by the increase in gross profit and a strong performance from the company&#8217;s Ardent Mills joint venture.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Adjusted EBITDA, which includes equity method investment earnings and pension and postretirement non-service income,&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x5" data-tblname="263861" data-tblv="20" id="led263861F2022791660051274036">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x4" data-tblname="263861" data-tblv="20" id="led263861F2022791660051283076">9.1%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="263861" data-tblv="20" id="led263861F2022791660051294195">$547</a> million in the quarter, primarily driven by the increase&nbsp;in adjusted gross profit and a strong performance from the company&#8217;s Ardent Mills joint venture, slightly offset by lower pension income.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Grocery &amp; Snacks Segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="53x1" data-tblname="263810" data-tblv="20" id="led263810F2022681657299999539">First Quarter</a> Results</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Reported and organic net sales for the Grocery &amp; Snacks segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="10x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F2022791660051335237">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="10x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F2022791660051343571">10.5%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="10x1" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F2022791660051355324">$1.2</a> billion in the quarter.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">In the quarter, price/mix&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="14x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20227181660834514519">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="14x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20227181660834530115">16.6%</a> and volume&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="13x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20227181660834548261">decreased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="13x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20227181660834559215">6.1%</a>. Price/mix was driven by favorability in inflation-driven pricing coupled with favorable brand mix. The volume decline was primarily due to the elasticity impact from inflation-driven pricing actions. In the q<font style="color:#333333;">uarter, the company gained share in snacking categories including meat snacks and microwave popcorn, and staples categories including syrup and Asian sauces and marinades.</font></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Operating profit for the segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x6" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835300580">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x4" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835314034">16.0%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835328717">$250</a> million in the quarter. Adjusted operating profit&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x6" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835351847">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x4" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835364347">15.4%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835378757">$254</a> million&nbsp;as higher organic net sales and supply chain realized productivity more than offset the&nbsp;negative impacts of cost of goods sold inflation, continued elevated supply chain operating&nbsp;costs, unfavorable operating leverage,&nbsp;and increased SG&amp;A.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Refrigerated &amp; Frozen Segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="53x1" data-tblname="263810" data-tblv="20" id="led263810F2022681657300003588">First Quarter</a> Results</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Reported and organic net sales for the Refrigerated &amp; Frozen segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="15x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20228131663088117935">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="15x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20228131663088127664">9.6%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="15x1" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20228131663088149020">$1.2</a> billion in the quarter.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">In the quarter, price mix&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="19x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20227181660845796630">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="19x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20227181660845814175">12.1%</a> and volume&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="18x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20227181660845828718">decreased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="18x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20227181660845838199">2.5%</a>. The price/mix increase was driven by favorability in inflation-driven pricing. The volume decline was primarily due to the elasticity impact from inflation-driven pricing.<font style="color:#ff0000;"> </font><font style="color:#333333;">In the quarter, the company gained share in categories such as frozen single serve meals, plant-based protein, and frozen breakfast.</font></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Operating loss for the segment was&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="4x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835426566">$216</a> million in the quarter primarily driven by the impairment charges&nbsp;discussed in further detail below. Adjusted operating profit&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="5x6" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835439908">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="5x4" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835449131">8.0%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="5x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835460673">$176</a> million as higher organic net sales and supply chain realized productivity more than offset the negative impacts of cost of goods sold inflation, continued elevated supply chain operating costs,&nbsp;increased SG&amp;A, and unfavorable operating leverage.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>International Segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="53x1" data-tblname="263810" data-tblv="20" id="led263810F2022681657300008689">First Quarter</a> Results</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Net sales for the International segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="20x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20228131663087917870">decreased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="20x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20228131663087940696">1.3%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="20x1" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20228131663087957030">$234</a> million in the quarter reflecting:</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>

			</td>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">On an organic net sales basis, price/mix&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="25x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20227181660845865062">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="25x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20227181660845876742">8.4%</a> and volume&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="24x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20227181660845890712">decreased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="24x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20227181660845906102">7.4%</a>. The price/mix increase was driven by inflation-driven pricing. Volume decreased primarily due to the elasticity impact from inflation-driven pricing actions.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Operating profit for the segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="6x6" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835480363">decreased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="6x4" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835491457">21.2%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="6x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835507368">$27</a> million in the quarter. Adjusted operating profit&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="7x6" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835520838">decreased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="7x4" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835529870">21.4%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="7x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835541056">$27</a> million as the benefits from higher organic net sales and&nbsp;supply chain realized productivity&nbsp;were&nbsp;more than offset by the negative impact&nbsp;of cost of goods sold inflation and unfavorable operating leverage.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Foodservice Segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="53x1" data-tblname="263810" data-tblv="20" id="led263810F2022681657300012778">First Quarter</a> Results</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Reported and organic net sales for the Foodservice segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="26x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20227181660845944550">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="26x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20227181660845955102">14.6%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="26x1" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20227181660845972046">$275</a> million in the quarter.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">In the quarter, price/mix increased&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="30x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20227181660846051858">18.8%</a>&nbsp;and volume&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="29x6" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20227181660846017711">decreased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="29x4" data-tblname="263825" data-tblv="20" id="led263825F20227181660846029439">4.2%</a>. The price/mix increase was driven by favorability in inflation-driven pricing. The volume decline was primarily due to the elasticity impact from inflation-driven pricing actions.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Operating profit for the segment&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x6" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835558773">decreased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x4" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835567800">94.1%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="8x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835595723">$1</a> million and adjusted operating profit&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x6" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835613611">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x4" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835622376">5.5%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20227181660835631690">$22</a> million in the quarter as the benefits of higher organic net sales and supply chain realized productivity more than offset the impacts of cost of goods sold inflation,&nbsp;elevated supply chain operating costs, and unfavorable operating leverage.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Other&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="53x1" data-tblname="263810" data-tblv="20" id="led263810F2022681657300016886">First Quarter</a> Items</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">During the first quarter, the Company reorganized its reporting structure for certain brands within two reporting units in the Refrigerated &amp; Frozen segment to increase brand management efficiencies. In connection with those changes and in accordance with&nbsp;U.S. GAAP, the company also evaluated goodwill for impairment, resulting in $386&nbsp;million of goodwill and brand impairment charges in SG&amp;A expenses with $244&nbsp;million associated with the&nbsp;<i>Bird's Eye&nbsp;</i>brand name.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Corporate expenses&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="10x6" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20228131663089724781">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="10x4" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20228131663089737077">29.3%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="10x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20228131663089748565">$84</a> million in the qua<font style="color:#333333;">rter and adjuste</font>d corporate expense&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="11x6" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20228131663089764461">increased</a>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="11x4" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20228131663089773144">27.9%</a> to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="11x1" data-tblname="263837" data-tblv="20" id="led263837F20228131663089783848">$80</a> million in the quarter driven by increased incentive compensation compared to&nbsp;the prior year quarter.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Pension and post-retirement non-service income was&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x1" data-tblname="263814" data-tblv="20" id="led263814F20227181660846326307">$6</a> million in the quarter compared to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="9x2" data-tblname="263814" data-tblv="20" id="led263814F20227181660846339340">$16</a> million of income in the prior-year period.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">In the quarter, equity method investment earnings were&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="10x1" data-tblname="263814" data-tblv="20" id="led263814F20227181660846351987">$49</a> million. The&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="7x3" data-tblname="263814" data-tblv="20" id="led263814F20227181660846509156">$29</a> million&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="7x4" data-tblname="263814" data-tblv="20" id="led263814F20227181660846521132">increase</a> was primarily driven by favorable market conditions for the Ardent Mills joint venture, and the venture&#8217;s effective management through recent volatility in the wheat markets.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">In the quarter, the effective tax rate was&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="19x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F20227181660846611717">(22.8)%</a> compared to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="19x2" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F20227181660846626747">22.8%</a> in the prior-year period which was largely impacted by the non-deductible goodwill impairments mentioned above. The adjusted effective tax rate was&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="20x1" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F20227181660846645523">22.9%</a> compared to&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="20x2" data-tblname="263848" data-tblv="20" id="led263848F20227181660846654756">24.0%</a> in the prior-year period.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">In the quarter, the Company<font style="color:#333333;"> paid a dividend of $0.3125 per share.&nbsp;</font>The Company's first dividend at the increased rate of&nbsp;$0.33&nbsp;per share was paid shortly following quarter-end.&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Outlook</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The Company is reaffirming&nbsp;guidance provided on its fourth quarter fiscal 2022 earnings call and&nbsp;as detailed below. For the second quarter of fiscal 2023, the Company has planned for continued supply chain inefficiency tied to the dynamic operating environment and some incremental volume weakness tied to the new inflation-driven pricing that went into effect early in the quarter. Gross inflation (input cost inflation before the impacts of hedging and other sourcing benefits) is expected to continue but moderate through the remainder of the fiscal year, resulting in low-teen levels, and commodity relief is expected to be weighted towards the back half of the fiscal year. Despite a strong early performance from its joint venture, Ardent Mills, the Company is not planning for elevated performance to&nbsp;continue throughout the remainder of the fiscal year due to the volatile nature of the business.&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Definitions</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Organic net sales excludes, from reported net sales, the impacts of foreign exchange, divested businesses and acquisitions, as well as the impact of any 53<sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:pt">rd</sup> week. All references to changes in volume and price/mix throughout this release are on an organic net sales basis.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">References to adjusted items throughout this release refer to measures computed in accordance with GAAP less the impact of items impacting comparability. Items impacting comparability are income or expenses (and related tax impacts) that management believes have had, or are likely to have, a significant impact on the earnings of the applicable business segment or on the total corporation for the period in which the item is recognized, and are not indicative of the company&#8217;s core operating results. These items thus affect the comparability of underlying results from period to period.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">References to earnings before interest, taxes, depreciation, and amortization (EBITDA) refer to net income attributable to Conagra Brands before the impacts of discontinued operations, income tax expense (benefit), interest expense, depreciation, and amortization. References to adjusted EBITDA refer to EBITDA before the impacts of items impacting comparability.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>About Conagra Brands</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Conagra Brands, Inc. (NYSE: CAG), headquartered in Chicago, is one of North America's leading branded food companies. Guided by an entrepreneurial spirit, Conagra Brands combines a rich heritage of making great food with a sharpened focus on innovation. The company's portfolio is evolving to satisfy people's changing food preferences. Conagra's iconic brands, such as Birds Eye&#174;, Marie Callender's&#174;, Banquet&#174;, Healthy Choice&#174;, Slim Jim&#174;, Reddi-wip&#174;, and Vlasic&#174;, as well as emerging brands, including Angie's&#174; BOOMCHICKAPOP&#174;, Duke's&#174;, Earth Balance&#174;, Gardein&#174;, and Frontera&#174;, offer choices for every occasion. For more information, visit <u>www.conagrabrands.com</u>.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Note on Forward-Looking Statements</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">This document contains forward-looking statements within the meaning of the federal securities laws. These forward-looking statements are based on management's current expectations and are subject to uncertainty and changes in circumstances. Readers of this document should understand that these statements are not guarantees of performance or results. Many factors could affect our actual financial results and cause them to vary materially from the expectations contained in the forward-looking statements, including those set forth in this document. These risks, uncertainties, and factors include, among other things: the risk that the cost savings and any other synergies from the acquisition of Pinnacle Foods Inc. (the Pinnacle acquisition) may not be fully realized or may take longer to realize than expected; the risk that the Pinnacle acquisition may not be accretive within the expected timeframe or to the extent anticipated; the risks that the Pinnacle acquisition and related integration will create disruption to the Company and its management and impede the achievement of business plans; risks related to our ability to achieve the intended benefits of other recent acquisitions and divestitures; risks associated with general economic and industry conditions; risks associated with our ability to successfully execute our long-term value creation strategies; risks related to our ability to deleverage on currently anticipated timelines, and to continue to access capital on acceptable terms or at all; risks related to our ability to execute operating and restructuring plans and achieve targeted operating efficiencies from cost-saving initiatives, and to benefit from trade optimization programs; risks related to the effectiveness of our hedging activities and ability to respond to volatility in commodities; risks related to the Company's competitive environment and related market conditions; risks related to our ability to respond to changing consumer preferences and the success of our innovation and marketing investments; risks related to the ultimate impact of any product recalls and litigation, including litigation related to the lead paint and pigment matters, as well as any securities litigation, including securities class action lawsuits; risk associated with actions of governments and regulatory bodies that affect our businesses, including the ultimate impact of new or revised regulations or interpretations; risks related to the impact of the COVID-19 pandemic on our business, suppliers, consumers, customers and employees; risks related to our forecasts of consumer eat-at-home habits as the impacts of the COVID-19 pandemic abate; risks related to the availability and prices of supply chain resources, including raw materials, packaging, and transportation including any negative effects caused by changes in inflation rates, weather conditions, or health pandemics or outbreaks of disease, actual or threatened hostilities or war, or other geopolitical uncertainty; disruptions or inefficiencies in our supply chain and/or operations, including from the COVID-19 pandemic; risks related to disruptions in the global economy caused by the ongoing conflict between Russia and Ukraine; risks associated with actions by our customers, including changes in distribution and purchasing terms; risks and uncertainties associated with intangible assets, including any future goodwill or intangible assets impairment charges; risks related to a material failure in or breach of our or our vendors&#8217; information technology systems; the amount and timing of future dividends, which remain subject to Board approval and depend on market and other conditions; risks related to the Company's ability to execute on its strategies or achieve expectations related to environmental, social, and governance matters, including as a result of evolving legal, regulatory, and other standards, processes, and assumptions, the pace of scientific and technological developments, increased costs, the availability of requisite financing, and changes in carbon markets, and other risks described in our reports filed from time to time</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>Note on Non-GAAP Financial Measures</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">This document includes certain non-GAAP financial measures, including adjusted EPS, organic net sales, adjusted gross profit, adjusted operating profit, adjusted SG&amp;A, adjusted corporate expenses, adjusted gross margin, adjusted operating margin, adjusted effective tax rate, adjusted net income attributable to Conagra Brands, free cash flow, net debt, net leverage ratio, and adjusted EBITDA. Management considers GAAP financial measures as well as such non-GAAP financial information in its evaluation of the Company&#8217;s financial statements and believes these non-GAAP measures provide useful supplemental information to assess the Company&#8217;s operating performance and financial position. These measures should be viewed in addition to, and not in lieu of, the Company&#8217;s diluted earnings per share, operating performance and financial measures as calculated in accordance with GAAP.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Certain of these non-GAAP measures, such as organic net sales, adjusted operating margin, and adjusted EPS, are forward-looking. Historically, the Company has excluded the impact of certain items impacting comparability, such as, but not limited to, restructuring expenses, the impact of the extinguishment of debt, the impact of foreign exchange, the impact of acquisitions and divestitures, hedging gains and losses, impairment charges, the impact of legacy legal contingencies, and the impact of unusual tax items, from the non-GAAP financial measures it presents. Reconciliations of these forward-looking non-GAAP financial measures to the most directly comparable GAAP financial measures are not provided because the Company is unable to provide such reconciliations without unreasonable effort, due to the uncertainty and inherent difficulty of predicting the occurrence and the financial impact of such items impacting comparability and the periods in which such items may be recognized. For the same reasons, the Company is unable to address the probable significance of the unavailable information, which could be material to future results.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">Hedge gains and losses are generally aggregated, and net amounts are reclassified from unallocated corporate expense to the operating segments when the underlying commodity or foreign currency being hedged is expensed in segment cost of goods sold. The Company identifies these amounts as items that impact comparability within the discussion of unallocated Corporate results.</p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 8pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:pt">1 </sup>Operating profit is derived from taking Income from continuing operations before income taxes and equity method investment earnings, adding back Interest expense, net and removing Pension and postretirement non-service income.</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 8pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:pt">2</sup> Advertising and promotion expense (A&amp;P) has been removed from adjusted selling, general and administrative expense because this metric is used in reporting to management, and management believes this adjusted measure provides useful supplemental information to assess the Company&#8217;s operating performance.&nbsp; Please note that A&amp;P is not removed from adjusted profit measures.</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 8pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:pt">3</sup> In Q1 FY23, we reported a GAAP net loss. In periods when we recognize a net loss, we exclude the impact of outstanding stock awards from the diluted loss per share calculation, as their inclusion would have an anti-dilutive effect. The adjusted diluted earnings per share calculation includes the impact of outstanding stock awards.</p>
